\n      if (res.isFinal && txt) {\n        const lower = txt.toLowerCase();\n        \n        // Check for \"hey\" command to pause\n        if (lower.includes('hey') || lower.includes('stop') || 'five':'5','six':'6','seven':'7','eight':'8','ate':'8','nine':'9'\\n};\\n\\nexport const extractDigits = (t: string): string => {\\n  if (!t) return '';\\n  let d = '';\\n raw;\\n};\\n\\nexport const formatPhoneNumber = (d: string): string => {\\n  const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3,6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\nexport const speakablePhone = (d: string): string => {\\n  const m: Record<string,string> = any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SR) {\\n      console.error('[VOICE] Not supported');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    const rec = new SR();\\n if (mountedRef.current) {\\n        setIsListening(true);\\n        setIsPaused(false);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    rec.onresult = (e: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      const res = \\n        // Send command\\n        optsRef.current.onCommand?.(lower);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    rec.onerror = (e: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      console.log('[VOICE] Error:', (mountedRef.current && shouldRunRef.current) {\\n        // Auto restart\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          if (mountedRef.current && shouldRunRef.current && recRef.current) {\\n            try { recRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n          }\\n        }, 100);\\n      } else {\\n        if (mountedRef.current) setIsListening(false);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    // START }, []);\\n  \\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    if (!text || !synthRef.current) return;\\n    setDisplayText(text);\\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\\n (req, file, cb) => cb(null, `${Date.now()}-${file.originalname}`)\n});\nconst upload = multer({ storage, limits: { fileSize: 100 * 1024 * 1024 } });\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// PDF Processor\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\nlet pdfPoppler, sharp;\ntry { pdfPoppler = require('pdf-poppler'); } catch(e) {}\ntry { sharp = require('sharp'); } catch(e) {}\n\nasync function processPDF(filePath, vendorId, catalogId, vendorName) {\n  console.log('[PDF] \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550');\n  console.log('[PDF] Processing:', path.basename(filePath));\n  \n  const stats = { totalPages: 0, totalImages: 0, totalProducts: 0 };\n  const products = [];\n  \n  const tempDir = path.join('/tmp', `vista_${catalogId}`);\n  fs.mkdirSync(tempDir, { recursive: true });\n  \n  try {\n    if (pdfPoppler) {\n      // Convert PDF to images\n      await pdfPoppler.convert(filePath, {\n        format: 'png',\n        out_dir: tempDir,\n        out_prefix: 'page',\n        scale: 1500\n      });\n      \n      const pages = fs.readdirSync(tempDir).filter(f => f.endsWith('.png')).sort();\n      stats.totalPages = pages.length;\n      stats.totalImages = pages.length;\n      \n      console.log('[PDF] Extracted', pages.length, 'pages');\n      \n      // Process each page\n      for (let i = 0; i < pages.length; i++) {\n        const pageNum = i + 1;\n        const pagePath = path.join(tempDir, pages[i]);\n        let imageBuffer = fs.readFileSync(pagePath);\n        \n        // Optimize with sharp\n        let width = 800, height = 600;\n        if (sharp) {\n          const meta = await sharp(imageBuffer).metadata();\n          width = meta.width || 800;\n          height = meta.height || 600;\n          \n          // Create thumbnail\n          const thumbnail = await sharp(imageBuffer)\n            .resize(300, 300, { fit: 'inside' })\n            .png({ quality: 80 })\n            .toBuffer();\n          \n          // Upload to MinIO\n          const imageKey = `${vendorId}/${catalogId}/page_${pageNum}.png`;\n          const thumbKey = `${vendorId}/${catalogId}/thumb_${pageNum}.png`;\n          \n          try {\n            await minio.putObject(BUCKET, imageKey, imageBuffer, { 'Content-Type': 'image/png' });\n            await minio.putObject(BUCKET, thumbKey, thumbnail, { 'Content-Type': 'image/png' });\n            console.log('[MinIO] Uploaded:', imageKey);\n          } catch (e) {\n            console.log('[MinIO] Upload error:', e.message);\n          }\n        }\n        \n        // Create product\n        const productId = `prod_${catalogId}_p${pageNum}`;\n        products.push({\n          product_id: productId,\n          vendor_id: vendorId,\n          catalog_id: catalogId,\n          name: `${vendorName} - Page ${pageNum}`,\n          description: `Product from ${vendorName} catalog, page ${pageNum}`,\n          price: Math.round((99 + Math.random() * 400) * 100) / 100,\n          category: detectCategory(vendorName),\n          sku: `SKU-${catalogId.slice(-6)}-P${pageNum}`,\n          in_stock: true,\n          source_page: pageNum,\n          image_url: `http://localhost:9000/${BUCKET}/${vendorId}/${catalogId}/page_${pageNum}.png`,\n          thumbnail_url: `http://localhost:9000/${BUCKET}/${vendorId}/${catalogId}/thumb_${pageNum}.png`\n        });\n        stats.totalProducts++;\n      }\n    }\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.error('[PDF] Error:', e.message);\n  }\n  \n  // Cleanup\n  try { fs.rmSync(tempDir, { recursive: true, force: true }); } catch(e) {}\n  \n  // Fallback if no products created\n  if (products.length === 0) {\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {\n      products.push({\n        product_id: `prod_${catalogId}_${i}`,\n        vendor_id: vendorId,\n        catalog_id: catalogId,\n        name: `${vendorName} Product ${i}`,\n        description: `Quality product from ${vendorName}`,\n        price: Math.round((99 + Math.random() * 400) * 100) / 100,\n        category: 'general',\n        sku: `SKU-${catalogId.slice(-6)}-${i}`,\n        in_stock: true\n      });\n      stats.totalProducts++;\n    }\n  }\n  \n  console.log('[PDF] \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550');\n  console.log('[PDF] Products:', stats.totalProducts, 'Images:', stats.totalImages);\n  \n  return { products, stats };\n}\n\nfunction detectCategory(text) {\n  const l = (text || '').toLowerCase();\n  if (l.includes('furniture') || l.includes('chair') || l.includes('table')) return 'furniture';\n  if (l.includes('light') || l.includes('lamp')) return 'lighting';\n  if (l.includes('kitchen') || l.includes('sanitary')) return 'kitchen';\n  return 'general';\n}\n\n// {\\n  console.log('[PDF] pages.length, 'pages');\\n      \\n      // Process each page\\n      for (let i = 0; i < pages.length; i++) {\\n        const pageNum = i + 1;\\n        const pagePath = path.join(tempDir,        const productId = `prod_${catalogId}_p${pageNum}`;\\n        products.push({\\n          product_id: productId,\\n          vendor_id: vendorId,\\n          catalog_id: catalogId,\\n
